Dumping of Japanese Light Bulbs

Shanghai Electrical Appliance Merchants Petition in Beijing 113

Successful Result, Representatives Return to Shanghai

According to Shanghai News Agency, Hu Xiyuan, the representative of the Chinese electrical appliance manufacturers who petitioned in Beijing, took the night train to Beijing on the 18th. At 2:00 PM on the 19th, he went to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to meet with Minister Chen Gongbo. He requested that the Ministry consult with the Ministry of Finance to draft regulations for an anti-dumping tax on Japanese light bulb imports and to announce and implement them as soon as possible to give domestic light bulbs a chance to survive. He also detailed the current dire situation of domestic light bulb sales, which have been severely affected by Japanese dumping. Minister Chen agreed to send personnel to Shanghai for investigation and then work with the Ministry of Finance to draft a tax rate for anti-dumping duties on Japanese-made light bulbs. Hu, satisfied with the response, immediately took the night train back to Shanghai on the 19th and reported the details of the Beijing petition to various manufacturers in writing at around 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon.

Special District Courts Jointly Establish Bonus System for Clerks 114

Those Who Are Honest and Diligent Without Fault Will Receive Awards

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch · Shanghai First Special District Local Court · Jointly Issued Public Notice No. 1371: For the matter of a public notice, it has been found that court clerks often engage in corrupt practices. The main reason is that their salaries are too low. Those with larger families find it difficult to support themselves in ordinary times, and even more so when they encounter weddings, funerals, or illnesses. Because court clerks have limited education and are exposed to many external temptations, they often seek illicit gains when given the opportunity, violating strict prohibitions. While their behavior should be severely punished, the underlying motivation should also be addressed. In light of this, the two courts have jointly established ten articles for a bonus system for court clerks. Any clerk who is honest, diligent, and without fault will receive a monthly bonus, which is tantamount to increasing their salary. The bonus will also be deposited and accrue interest, providing security for unforeseen circumstances, similar to labor insurance. However, the stored bonus cannot be withdrawn at will. If corrupt practices are discovered, the entire amount will be confiscated. With years of accumulated savings at stake, who would risk a small gain for a significant loss? This is a combination of reward and punishment, hoping to guide them towards repentance and improvement. It is hoped that this is understood by all. The established system will be implemented from January 1st of this year. This public notice is hereby issued for general information. The ten articles of the court clerk bonus system are listed below for the benefit of all court clerks and litigants of both courts. This notice includes: Court Clerk Bonus System, ㈠ The court has established a court clerk bonus to encourage honesty and diligence among court clerks. ㈡ Clerks who are honest, diligent, and without fault will receive a bonus of four to six yuan per month in addition to their original salary. ㈢ The bonus to be received by the clerk will be deposited monthly by the General Affairs Office into the Postal Savings Bureau to accrue interest. All withdrawals will require the signature of the General Affairs Office. The clerk can hold the bonus passbook, but it cannot be used to borrow money. ㈣ If a clerk commits a minor fault, the bonus for that month will be reduced accordingly. If corrupt practices are discovered that damage the court's reputation, such as accepting bribes, tips, or engaging in fraudulent activities, they will be severely punished according to law, and all accumulated bonuses will be confiscated. ㈤ All confiscated bonuses will be deposited by the General Affairs Office into a separate account as a special award fund. ㈥ Clerks who refuse to accept bribes or tips from litigants and immediately report it will be given a special bonus based on the circumstances. ㈦ Clerks who see other clerks accepting bribes or tips and immediately report it will be given a special bonus based on the circumstances. The names of the informants will be kept confidential by the responsible personnel. ㈧ If a clerk needs funds urgently due to a major event such as a wedding, funeral, or illness, they may request an advance on a portion of their stored bonus, but it must be verified by the General Affairs Office and reviewed by the Chief Clerk before being issued. ㈨ When a clerk resigns or leaves the court, except for those dismissed for corruption, the stored bonus, principal, and interest will be returned in full. ㈩ This system will be implemented from January 1, 1933. President of the Court Shen Jia · President of the Court Guo Yunguan · January 19, 1933, Republic of China.

Thief Active in Cinema 118

丨Stealing Three Hats, Sentenced to Two Years丨

The thief, Shen Guanbao, a native of Guangdong, is 27 years old this year. On the 19th, he went to the Paris Cinema on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession under the pretext of watching a movie. Taking advantage of the darkness, he stole three felt hats from under the seats. He was noticed by the owners, Guo Shaorong, Jin Shaokong, and a Russian named Xin Gaseski, who caught Shen and handed him over to the police. Yesterday, he was sent to the Simple Court of the Second Special District. The police lawyer, Chen Ming, first explained the case, stating that the defendant had been sentenced to one year in prison by the First Special Court for theft last year and has committed another offense. He requested that he be severely investigated. When questioned, Shen Guanbao confessed that he was forced to commit this illegal act due to economic hardship and asked for leniency. Judge Zhang sentenced Shen Guanbao, alias Sun Guifang, to two years of imprisonment for repeated theft.

Fire on the Bund of the South City 119

At 9:30 PM the night before last, a fire broke out at the back of the Tongshun Gongji Oil Basket Shop at No. 516 and the Xiafutai Secondhand Goods Shop at No. 515 on the Bund of the South City, near the Xinmatou Street. The fire suddenly broke through the roof and spread to Li Qingrong's residence on the upper floor of No. 514 and the Fajji Shipping Company on the lower floor. It also affected the rear building of Yu Zu_ 's house at No. 510. Fortunately, police officer Ma Tingzhen immediately reported to the fire brigades of the South City, who dispatched fire trucks to the scene and worked hard to extinguish the fire. The fire was finally put out at midnight. At that time, the neighbors nearby heard the alarm and rushed to grab boxes and luggage, causing temporary chaos. The district chief of the first district, Guan Gong Li, and the police rushed to the scene to suppress the situation and maintain order. They also summoned Qiu Bokun, the manager of Tongshun Oil Basket Shop, and Zhang Xuezhong, the old clerk of Xiafutai, to the district for questioning. Qiu and Zhang both shirked responsibility and denied starting the fire. District Chief Guan ordered them to be temporarily detained and investigated further. It is said that Xiafutai had taken out fire insurance worth 2,000 taels with Dahua Company.

The Longda Steamer of the Shenyang Class at Datong Pier in the South City discovered a male corpse in the rear of the cargo hold just as it was about to set sail the night before last. Wuchang Steamer Steward Delivered Gold Bars and Never Returned 123

Worth More Than 98,400 Yuan

The Carrier Has Been Detained on Suspicion

Zou Shunjin, a native of Ningbo, has been transporting gold bars for various silver shops in the port for more than ten years. This time, he took the Taikoo Company's Wuchang Steamer from Hankou to Shanghai, transporting a total of 18 flat (each flat weighing more than 50 taels) of pure gold for various silver shops, worth more than 98,400 yuan. The ship arrived at the port at 2:15 PM on the 16th and docked at the company's pier north of _ Nidu, Pudong. Zou entrusted Chen Rongcai, the steward of the ship, to deliver it to Yangqinghe Silver Shop in the port and transfer it to various cargo owners. Zou first took a head ferry to Pu and waited at the silver shop. Unexpectedly, by 6:00 PM that evening, Chen had not delivered the gold. Zou immediately returned to the ship and asked other stewards. They said that Chen had taken the head ferry to Pu at 3:30 PM. Zou knew that something was wrong and immediately reported to the silver shops and sent people to search everywhere, but there was no trace of him. It was not until 9:00 PM on the 17th that Zou reported to the Customs Water Patrol Station, requesting _ to arrest him. According to Zou, he has been doing this for more than ten years, receiving 3 yuan per flat, and there has never been an accident. After the gold arrived in Shanghai, he has always entrusted Chen Rongcai, who is now at large, to deliver it ashore, giving him 5 jiao per flat. He trusted that Chen was honest and reliable and never changed him. He did not expect this sudden evil act, which was completely unexpected. The patrol station believed that Zou had a heavy responsibility and was in a suspicious position, so he was detained. Detectives were sent to investigate, but after three days, there was still no clue. It was assumed that the suspect had already left Shanghai, so the news was released to the public yesterday. As for the silver shops that were harmed and the amount of loss, they are listed below: ㈠ Dadecheng at No. 63 Fuxing Lane, Beijing Road, entrusted to carry two flat, weighing 118 taels and 7 fen, ㈡ Laofengxiang at No. 356 Nanjing Road, three flat, weighing 163 taels, 1 qian, and 3 fen, ㈢ Yuanfeng at No. 21 Xiamen Road, flat, weighing 51 taels and 5 qian, ㈣ Tongfengyong at No. 182 Nanjing Road, four flat, weighing 224 taels, 7 qian, and 2 fen, ㈤ Tongfu at No. 10 Renmei Lane, Ningbo Road, three flat, weighing 151 taels and 1 qian, ㈥ Wuxingcheng at No. 447 A, Liugui Lane, North Zhejiang Road, two flat, weighing 123 taels and 4 qian, ㈦ Yongcheng at No. 96 Beijing Road, one flat, weighing 54 taels, 3 qian, and 4 fen.

Li Guojie's Appeal 124

=Li Xiwang Is Still Receiving Treatment in Shanghai=

=The Local Court Must Ask the High Court for Instructions=

Li Guojie, the former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was sentenced to three years of imprisonment by the Shanghai Local Court for the case of fraudulently borrowing foreign debts with Chen Fumu by misappropriating the property of the China Merchants Bureau. Li was sent to the hospital because he was ill. Li Guojie's lawyer has now written an appeal and appealed to the Suzhou High Court of the second instance. The Shanghai Local Court has sent the entire file to Suzhou for review. However, Li requested the court to remain in the Shanghai Hospital for treatment due to illness. The court stated that the appeal case has been sent to Suzhou and cannot make a decision and will wait to be submitted to the High Court for review.

Revival of Macau Lottery in Shanghai 125

One Hundred and Twenty Characters with Ten Winning Characters

Shanghai Gamblers Flock to It

Cantonese Man Zhang Zhongqia Manages It in Shanghai

Arrested Twice, Requesting Strict Handling

|Defendant Plans to Appeal After Trial|

A type of Macau lottery was issued in this city ten years ago, which was once very popular, but was later banned by the authorities. Recently, it has been revived and is prevalent in the Hongkou area, with most gamblers being Cantonese. It is understood that the general office of the lottery is located in Macau, with a grand scale, and has operating branches in various countries. The lottery method is that the headquarters selects 120 characters, and the lottery is drawn every ten days, with ten characters out of the 120 being the winning numbers. Gamblers select ten characters each time, and if the ten characters selected are exactly the same as the ones drawn, they can win a bonus of several thousand yuan for every yuan bet. Even matching some of the characters can result in a large bonus. Seeing such large bonuses, general gamblers believe they can become rich overnight, so they flock to it. The representative of the Shanghai operating branch is Zhang Zhongqia (also known as Zhang De), the owner of the Yuelai Cantonese Food Store at 586 Wuchang Road, who is Cantonese. This matter was learned by Yao Jialin, the Chinese Detective Chief of District C of the Public Concession Police, who went on the tenth of last month to arrest Zhang, along with lottery tickets, and handed them over to the First Special Court. On the eleventh, Zhang was sentenced to two months imprisonment and fined 120 yuan. Zhang refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the collegiate bench of the Special Court, but the appeal was rejected. However, because Zhang was a first-time offender, the sentence was suspended for two years. After Zhang was released from prison, he still did not repent and continued to operate this gambling lottery as before. Unexpectedly, Yao the Detective Chief found out again, reported to the Special Court, and obtained a search warrant. At 6 p.m. the day before yesterday, he led police officers to search the premises. At that time, Zhang was writing lottery tickets with his partner, Cantonese man Zhang Yifen. Yao arrested them, confiscated many lottery tickets and money, and took them back to the Hongkou Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu filed a lawsuit in accordance with Article 280 of the Criminal Law, and stated that although the defendant Zhang Zhongqia was nominally operating the Yuelai Food Store, the store was just a front, and his only productive capacity was actually operating the lottery. Although he had been arrested last time, the court sentence was too light, so the defendant did not know shame and continued to operate as before. Unexpectedly, he was caught by the police again. Therefore, he requested the court to impose a severe penalty to serve as a warning to others. Following this, Detective Chief Yao Jialin submitted a report detailing the circumstances of the seizure, and explained in detail the usage of the seized lottery tickets, etc. When questioned, Zhang Zhongyi denied operating a gambling lottery. Zhang Yifen confessed without denial. Judge Liu Gui verified the confession and immediately pronounced the judgment: Zhang Zhongyi was sentenced to four months imprisonment and fined 200 yuan; Zhang Yifen was sentenced to two months imprisonment and fined 80 yuan. If the fines were not paid, they would be converted into imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. After the sentencing, the defendants declared they would appeal and requested permission to post bail. The court then ordered that each be allowed to post 600 yuan bail during the appeal period and await further trial outside the court.

Publish an advertisement requesting purchasers of the ticket to return their stubs by the deadline. A summary notice is appended as follows: This office previously distributed charity race lottery tickets to various parties for sale, all sent out in complete books, each book with a ticket stub. Now, as we are concluding matters, we have discovered that a small number of lottery tickets were sold along with the ticket stubs, making recovery impossible. We hereby announce this to the public. All sectors who have purchased lottery tickets with the ticket stub attached must detach the stub and return it to the original point of sale before the 23rd of this month for forwarding to this office, or send it directly to this office and the Shanghai Race Club by registered mail. This measure is strictly to avoid future disputes. We hope that purchasers of tickets holding stubs will take note.

Municipal Government Commends Inland Water Company 126

Awards Certificate of Merit

Central News Agency reports that since the beginning of the 18th year of the Republic, the Municipal Public Works Bureau formulated a reform plan for the city's inland water company, ordering the company to carry out improvements accordingly. In February of that year, the company first ordered four sets each of raw water electric pumps and clean water electric pumps. In September, it built two coagulation sedimentation tanks and six rapid filter tanks, with a daily water output of more than 45,000 cubic meters. It also added two clean water tanks with a capacity of approximately 17,700 cubic feet, a water tower with a capacity of approximately 286 cubic meters, and other projects such as raw water wells, alum water tanks, raw water machines, adjustment tanks, transformer stations, main water gate rooms, meter rooms, etc., all of which were completed in the autumn of the 20th year. All original steam engines and alum water tanks before the 18th year were immediately shut down. The total capital increase for various reconstruction, additions and installations, and the purchase of large pipe water meters, etc., amounted to approximately 2 million yuan. Since then, the water quality, water volume, and water pressure have all significantly improved, and the citizens of South Shanghai can often enjoy clean and sufficient drinking water. At the same time, internal organization and administration have also been greatly reformed, washing away accumulated bad habits. Therefore, last month, the Municipal Public Works Bureau requested the Municipal Government to issue a commendation. The Municipal Government specially issued a certificate of merit yesterday as follows: "The Inland Water Company has improved its equipment, fully supplying clean drinking water, benefiting the citizens, and has made meritorious contributions to construction. It is deeply commendable. This certificate is hereby awarded."

Sunken Ship from Forty Years Ago Discovered at the Mouth of the Yangtze River 128

〓Obstructs Waterway〓

〓Notify River Vessels〓

The Hydrographic Office of the Ministry of the Navy issued a notice informing all vessels navigating the Yangtze River, stating that the hull of the sunken vessel Anwo, which sank 16 years before the founding of the Republic, had been discovered at the mouth of the Yangtze River. During low water, the upper half of the sunken vessel is exposed on the river surface, while during high tide it cannot be seen. It is understood that since the ship sank, it has been nearly 40 years. Now it has suddenly been discovered in the Yangtze River, and it is sufficient to obstruct the waterway. All river vessels have been notified to be careful to avoid it, so as to avoid accidents.

Extra Shifts Added to City Ferries During Year-End Closing Period 129

And Extended Service Hours for Donglu Route Ferry

The Municipal Ferry, which is run by the Municipal Public Works Bureau, has recently seen a sudden surge in passengers due to the approaching year-end closing date for businesses, resulting in the existing shifts being insufficient to cope with the demand. It is also reported that the cross-river ferry from Dongmen Road to Lujia Ferry will extend its service hours to midnight on January 25th to meet the demand.

Bids for Tea and Snacks on Shanghai-Hangzhou Line Passenger Cars Opened Yesterday 132

Xu Shuchen Wins the Bid

The tea and snack service on the passenger cars of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines has always been contracted out to merchants. The contract for the tea and snack service on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line passenger cars has now expired. In order to prevent private malfeasance, the bureau has publicly advertised for bids. It is reported that the bids were opened publicly in the conference room of the Railway Bureau at 11:00 a.m. yesterday. In addition to the audience and bidders, Bureau Chief Huang Boqiao presided over the meeting. Those present included the department-appointed resident auditor of the railway, Lin Zezheng, Chen Chengshi, executive member of the special party department of the two railways, Chen Fuhai, member of the supervisory committee, Huang Heng, chief of the general affairs department, Yuan Boyang, deputy chief, and Zheng Baozhao, chief of the traffic department. Auditor Lin executed the opening of the bids. A total of eight bids were received. The annual car rental offered was: Xu Xingquan, 2,830 yuan; Xu Shuchen, 3,550 yuan; Yan Fuchen, 3,250 yuan; Wang Fusheng, 2,700 yuan; Li Xiulin, 2,660 yuan; Ni Rongjin, 2,820 yuan; Yang Bin, 2,520 yuan; and Shen Bofan, 1,360 yuan. According to the regulations, Xu Shuchen, who offered the highest bid, won the bid. The chairman, auditor, executive committee member of the party department, supervisory committee member, and traffic department chief all jointly signed the bid form to show their prudence.

French Army Commander Lucamde to Arrive in Shanghai Today 133

The Shanghai Times reports that Colonel Lucamde, the newly appointed French commander of the army stationed in various parts of China, is coming to China to take office on the French mail steamer Andes Laming, and will arrive in Shanghai tomorrow morning (January 21). The French authorities and French nationals in this city are currently preparing a welcome. The commander's subsequent itinerary is not yet known. He will probably stay in Shanghai for a week to visit friends, and then go to Tianjin to take office, where his credentials and commissions have been sent, as Tianjin is where the French army headquarters is located.

Qingchang Small Ferry Resumes Service 134

The Qingchang inland river ferry between Qingyang Port and Changre, which was previously suspended due to the severe cold weather and freezing of the river surface, as noted in this newspaper on the 18th, has resumed service this morning after the recent heavy snow and the slight warming of the climate, with the ice on the river melting along with the accumulated snow. The company has decided to resume service this morning to maintain transportation during the end-of-year period. It is also reported that the Beijing-Shanghai Station in this city will also resume normal sales of through passenger tickets to Changre this morning.

Reward Offered for Arrest of Murderers of Petitioning Police Officer 135

Shi Xundong, a patrol officer stationed by the Fourth District of the Municipal Police Bureau at the International Telegraph Office, was patrolling by motorcycle around 11 p.m. on December 22nd of last year when he encountered bandits near Tangqiao and a fight broke out. Officer Shi was shot in a vital area by the bandits and died. However, the case has not yet been solved. Wen Hongen, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, yesterday issued a notice No. 4, offering a reward for the arrest of the fugitives.

Died for a Small Profit 136

Zhao Pi Died Pathetically

The Yisheng ship of Jardine Matheson Company was berthed at the China Merchants Wharf. At 2:30 p.m. yesterday, the ship had already left the wharf by about three feet when Zhao Pi, a 37-year-old Tianjin native who was the ship's supervisor, was greedy for a small profit. Because the price of silver dollars in Shanghai was better than in other ports, he hurriedly took three silver dollars intending to go ashore to exchange them for copper coins, but lost his footing and fell into the water. Although a sampan managed to rescue him, he had already frozen to death. It was truly tragic.

Letter 141

Dear Editor, I have read the news item in your newspaper of January 20, entitled "Disputes in the North among Former Contractors of Hangzhou Passenger Car Tea and Snacks," and the details contained therein are completely inconsistent with the facts. Please correct them to avoid rumors. The workers of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway tea and snacks were oppressed by the subcontracting system of Xu Huisheng, the representative of Shunli Company, in 18 years of the Republic, which led to anti-subcontracting disputes. The parties signed an agreement. When the contract expired, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Tea and Snacks Association took over from the Railway Bureau. First, on July ____ 20th, an agreement was signed with the Bureau. on July of the 21st year the contract expired, A request was made for renewal, so the first contract was signed again in that year. At 4 p.m. that day, the representatives of the workers, Sun Wen ______, _______ Lin, Lu Yisheng, and three people, the Bureau _______, deputy head of, Business section head and and Chief tang signed to order the second contract, which approved by the head limited time of one year and ensured a deposit of 3,000 yuan (the deposit from the 20th to the 21st year was 1,666 yuan, 6 jiao, and 6 fen). After the full payment was made, the contract could be issued immediately. Then, on _____ month 24, The workers deposited the remaining 1,233 yuan, 3 jiao, and 4 fen, totaling 2,000 yuan, and the Business Section issued a receipt. Repeatedly sending people to request the issuance of a new contract. Department Chief Zheng of the Office repeatedly delayed the appointment. After the new Director Huang took office, he also went to the Traffic Department several times to Chief Zheng issued new contract. At first, it was said that the new director had not been in office for long and was busy with official duties, so we should wait a few days before it could be issued. Then, he made irresponsible excuses. Suddenly, on the 12th of this month, he advertised for bids. Then, on the 16th, the people Chief Zheng, Unexpectedly said that the new contract has not been signed, the deposit of 3,000 yuan can be returned, etc., is self-contradictory and evasive, showing that his methods are despicable and violent. May I ask that since the new contract has not been signed, how can the full deposit be collected? Whose fault is it? There should be public opinion. Therefore, many petitions were made later, but all were ineffective. On the morning of the 19th of this month, the workers, driven by livelihood, automatically led their wives and children to the Relief Office to petition again. 30 railway police officers were sent to drive away the petitioning women and children. After being informed, In addition to reporting to the two railway party departments, it was deeply feared that the dispute would escalate. Therefore, worker representatives Lu Jinkun, Mei Ruisheng, Qian Zuhong, etc. were sent to persuade the workers to return home and wait quietly for a solution. Unexpectedly, the railway police mistakenly identified the three representatives as instigators and detained them at the police station and transferred them to the Public Security Bureau. Therefore, the battle situation described in your newspaper is largely untrue. The matter is of great importance, so I am writing to request a correction. This letter is addressed to the Shenbao Newspaper Office. Sincerely, The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Tea and Snacks Association.

Dear Editor, I have just read the news item in your newspaper's local news column, entitled "Former Contractors of Shanghai-Hangzhou Passenger Car Tea and Snacks Disturbed in the North", which contained the following statements: "Sun Wenpin, who claims to be the manager of the Shanghai-Hangzhou passenger car tea and snacks, and dozens of family members of the workers he hired, stormed into the office of the chief of the Traffic Department, demanding the cancellation of the bidding" and "It is said that Sun Wenpin's contract for the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway tea and snacks expired in July of last year, and former Director Chen Xinghan approved the continuation of the contract and ordered a deposit of 3,000 yuan to be paid in advance, pending review and approval. However, this matter has not yet been determined, and Sun Wenpin has already posted an advertisement claiming to be the contractor, which is close to deception." The above is not consistent with the facts. The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway tea and snacks business has always been contracted by the former Tea and Snacks Cooperative (now renamed the Tea and Snacks Association). After being publicly elected by the members, I am the representative of the masses, not an individual contractor. I have never used my personal name to post an advertisement claiming to be the contractor, which can be verified and need not be elaborated on. As for the petition to the Traffic Department by the workers and their families yesterday, it was also driven by livelihood and has been investigated and dealt with by the association. The matter concerns my reputation, and I should write to your newspaper to request a quick correction. This is addressed to Mr. Editor of the Shenbao Newspaper Office. Sincerely, Sun Wenpin.

Reader's Advisor

The Problem of the "Panic Cycle Law" 142

丨Letter from Mr. Wang Xiping丨

In your esteemed newspaper, Mr. Nai mentioned the problem of the "panic cycle law" in a previous current affairs commentary, including the following words: "The theory of prosperity and decline is not only embraced by our country's ancient sages, but also regarded as a fundamental truth by Western economists, namely the so-called panic cycle law. We do not wish to fundamentally deny the panic cycle law, but only to modify it." When I read this passage, I felt a bit doubtful in my heart. Because according to Mr. Nai's meaning, the panic cycle law advocated by European economists is mostly the same as the so-called "cycle" of our country's ancient sages, and now we need Mr. Nai of China to modify it on their behalf, changing the "merry-go-round" panic cycle theory into a "spiral" panic cycle theory. In fact, the facts are not like this, so I raise this question, intending to remind Mr. Nai that the panic cycle law referred to by Western economists is not only a "merry-go-round" type, but also a "spiral" type, and it seems that Mr. Nai does not need to modify it. It would be appreciated if Mr. Nai would elaborate and support it. I will introduce the materialistic dialectical panic cycle theory of Western economists below for reference, and note that it was published in "1894." However, due to other reasons, I could not immediately point out the author and book title. Later, your newspaper published this article, but deleted the above-mentioned important introductory text. At the same time, Mr. Nai's answer admitted that "orthodox economists believe that the panic cycle law is a merry-go-round type." The implication is that non-orthodox economists may also oppose this merry-go-round panic cycle theory, and I thought that was fine. Because the reader's consultant column is not a place where this kind of issue can be fully discussed. Today, I saw Mr. Nai's opinion on the question I raised last time from a friend, saying: "..." very meaningful, but the wording is quite unclear, probably because the author is busy. It would be quite interesting if the author could organize and re-present it for discussion." What exactly does "the wording is quite unclear" refer to? The panic cycle theory I introduced is entirely from the author's original text. Does "the wording is quite unclear" refer to my translation, or does it refer to the original text I translated? Moreover, I have not added any of my own opinions. Now, I will re-record the original text on this issue below for instruction: "Mr. Nai's conclusion on the panic cycle is very appropriate, but the theory of the panic cycle law published in 1894 is not as Mr. Nai said. Here is a brief introduction of the original text: "The statistics of exporters give a standard for the reality, that is, the accumulation of productive capital and commodity capital. And the statistics often indicate the following fact, that is, in the development period of the operation of British industry (1815 to 1870) in the ten-year cycle, each time at the highest limit of the last prosperous period of the panic, it is newly expressed as the lowest limit of the next prosperous period, and then rises to a higher new highest limit." Thus, a factual proof is given to us from the statistics: "The actual, i.e., declared, value of exports of British and Irish products in the prosperous period of 1814 was £40,396,300. Then the panic of 1825 brought the export volume below this total, fluctuating between 35 million and 39 million per year. Because of the recovery of the economy in 1834, the export volume rose again and exceeded the previous highest level, reaching £41,649,191, and reaching a new highest limit of £53,368,571 in 1836. Then, in 1837, the amount of exports was reduced to 42 million, so that the new lowest limit was already higher than the old highest limit, and then it fluctuated between 50 million and 53 million pounds. In 1844, the atmosphere recovered, thus raising the export volume to 58.5 million, that is, the highest limit of 1826 had already been far exceeded by this export volume. In 1845, the export volume reached £60,111,082; then in 1846, it was strong at £57 million, in 1847, it was about £59 million, in 1848, it was about £53 million, and in 1849, it rose to £63.5 million. In 1853, it was about 99 million, in 1849, it rose to 63.5 million, in 1853, it was about 99 million, in 1854, it was 97 million, in 1855, it was 54.5 million, in 1856, it was about 100.06 million, and in 1857, it reached the highest limit with 122 million. In 1858, the export volume was reduced to 111.6 million, but by 1859 it had risen to 130 million, in 1860 it was about 136 million, and in 1861 it was only 125 million (here, the new lowest limit was higher than the previous highest limit,) 146.65 million pounds in 1863 (same as above 丨 same page). " This development of the panic cycle is clearly not a "merry-go-round" type, but a "spiral" type; that is to say, it is not formalistic (it can also be said that it is not of the orthodox school of economics) but is a dialectical development of the negation of the negation to a higher level."...... The above paragraph, except that I deleted some words complimenting Mr. Nai and added the words "not of the orthodox school of economics," is all copied from the last original text. With my clumsy understanding, his explanation of the meaning of the panic cycle law is very clear, and there is no "unclear" place. The two footnotes I made are even more obvious. I don't know what exactly Mr. Nai means by "the wording is quite unclear". I respectfully request instruction. (Furthermore, the article introduced in this article is from page 29 of the first volume of the third volume of the German "Capital." If the discussion text is not convenient to publish in the newspaper, please reply by letter from Mr. Nai.)

Reporter's Note: Regarding the question of the "panic cycle law," Mr. Wang and his reply have aroused interest. Regarding the opinions stated in the letter on the right, if Mr. Nai of this newspaper believes that there is still room for discussion, in addition to continuing the discussion, readers are welcome to submit letters for discussion if they have any insightful opinions.

Few Elementary School Students Pass the Examination in Hangzhou City 147

▲202 Candidates, Only 50 Pass

▲Those Who Failed in One, Two, or Three Subjects Will Take a Make-up Exam Today

The first Hangzhou City Elementary School Graduation Examination was held at Tianchang Elementary School on the 16th. Of the 202 students who took the exam, only 50 passed each subject and were allowed to graduate. In addition, two students who failed the previous exam but retook the exam were allowed to graduate. Those who did not graduate, regardless of whether they failed one, two, or three subjects, will be allowed to take a retest at the Municipal Tianchang Elementary School starting at 9:00 a.m. today (the 21st). If they still fail, they will take a make-up exam at the next graduation examination.

Chen Kezhong Discusses the Overview of Inspecting Education in Fujian Province 150

The Ministry of Education previously sent Dr. Chen Kezhong, a full-time editor and reviewer of the National Compilation and Translation Hall, to inspect the education status of public and private secondary schools and above in Fuzhou and Xiamen, Fujian Province. Chen arrived in Fuzhou on the 22nd of last month, inspected for four weeks, and returned to Beijing on the evening of the 18th of this month. According to a conversation with Dr. Chen by reporters on the 19th, a summary of the inspection is as follows.

Chen's inspection situation, divided by location, includes four schools in Xiamen and twenty schools in Fuzhou. In terms of school level, it includes four higher education schools and twenty secondary education schools. (1) Higher Education: Xiamen University's science equipment is very good. The school and Jimei are both operated privately by Chen Jiageng. The rumor that Chen Jiageng is going bankrupt is not true. Chen Jiageng still subsidizes Xiamen University with 12,000 yuan per month and Jimei Middle School with 10,000 yuan per month. The provincial government has recently approved a subsidy of 60,000 yuan per year (5,000 per month) for the university, so it is unlikely to be shaken as rumored. This is one university. Also inspected were Fujian Union Theological College and South China Women's College (the above three colleges were changed from universities to colleges, and South China is a women's college). South China Women's College is the only highest women's education institution in Fujian, with a history of more than twenty years. It is well-managed, but it has not yet been officially registered. Union Theological College has complete facilities, especially the best science equipment, which is better than other famous universities in various places. After inspecting one university and three colleges, it is planned to cooperate and become a perfect university. Chen Kezhong and Zheng Zhenwen, the director of the Education Department, convened a meeting of university presidents, including Lin Wenqing, the president of Xiamen University, He Gonggan, the president of Fuzhou College, and Lin Jingrun, the president of Union Theological College, as well as the academic deans of each school. After joint design, the higher education institutions in Fujian will be divided into labor and cooperation, each focusing on the points and trends they have adopted, identifying goals, and handling them separately without repetition.

National Economic Commission Education Special Committee

Discussion on the Recommendations of the League of Nations Education Inspection Team (Part 2) 151

The original recommendation is as follows: A. An efficient teaching profession. The training of teachers must be reformed. All teachers in the country should have an equal standard determined by the state with regulations, and it is recommended that the state hold teacher examinations, starting with the examination of middle school teachers, and then to other stages. The salaries of teachers at all levels should be stipulated in accordance with a certain grade and must be paid on time. The lack of security in the teaching profession, that is, the instability of the teaching profession and the main reason for the reduction of efficiency. The number of university lectureships and teacher positions should be limited, but they must be stabilized. The appointment of teachers should be entirely based on qualifications. Only in cases of clear incompetence or for the purpose of warning can dismissal be permitted. Teachers should be appointed by the competent education authority and not by the principal.

Resolution (3) The points mentioned in the first section of the third item, establishing an efficient school system, can be sent to the Ministry of Education for reference.

Original Resolution Section 1 is as follows: An efficient school system. In order to build a truly efficient education system for the country, elementary education must be compulsory, and six years of education should be the goal, but in special circumstances in the locality, four years of compulsory education can also be recognized. Since compulsory education is implemented, elementary education must be free. All children who come to school do not pay fees. Elementary schools are the foundation of the education system. Under the current situation, the development of elementary schools in China is extremely important. The implementation of compulsory education must be investigated on the ground in pilot cities and counties and prepared with caution. Because elementary education is fundamentally important, the National Government and all provinces should allocate funds for this item. The Ministry of Education should set up a special elementary education department. Also, if the number of students taught by each teacher and each school is increased, the efficiency of the use of schools and teachers can be further increased.

Resolution (4) The points mentioned in the first, second, and third sections of the fourth item, establishing an efficient teaching method, can be formulated in detail by the Ministry of Education, and ordered the education halls and bureaus of each province and city to transfer the order to the schools at all levels under their jurisdiction to strictly follow.

Original Resolutions Sections 1, 2, and 3 are as follows:

Efficient Teaching

(1) All teachers must be proficient in the lessons they teach, and not just be proficient in their teaching methods. Basic research on history and psychology in education is certainly important, but this research should not obscure the teaching materials themselves.

(2) Teaching should rely less on textbooks and more on experiments and practical work (especially in science) and reference books (in history and language).

(3) The hours of lectures in all schools should be reduced, and the hours used in laboratories and manual labor should be increased.

(For example, A runs science, B runs science, and C runs education. The result of division of labor and cooperation is very unsatisfactory. 1) Secondary education: A total of 20 schools were inspected. The equipment for science and library is lacking (judging from the equipment that should be available according to the curriculum standards, there is too little. If we look at the modern equipment of general schools, they are also average). Some schools have too much political color and should be improved. With the Education Department planning to establish a public science museum in the near future to subsidize the inadequacy of the scientific equipment of each school, schools in the provincial capital can use it at any time. 3) The Civil Education Center is located in the park, which is not suitable. And the museum has all the equipment standards set by the Ministry of Education, but it fails to consider the actual situation of the locality when allocating equipment. It seems uneconomical.

Local News

Schools Should Adopt Textbooks Incorporating the New Metric System 153

▲The Municipal Education Bureau Recently Ordered All Schools to Comply

The Municipal Education Bureau previously approved the letter from the National Bureau of Weights and Measures of the Ministry of Industry requesting the promotion of the new metric system, and specifically ordered it to the schools in this city. The official letter from the National Bureau of Weights and Measures of the Ministry of Industry stated: "After investigation, the officialdom in our country is vast, and the weights and measures vary, resulting in rampant fraud and numerous harms, which have a profound impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood. It is imperative to formulate standards that the entire country can follow in order to eliminate malpractice and achieve unification. The National Government, in view of this, has successively promulgated the standards of weights and measures, as well as various subsidiary laws and regulations of the Republic of China, for compliance. Since its implementation, it has achieved remarkable results. At present, the provinces and cities along the Yangtze River and the coast have taken the lead in implementation, and the provinces in the interior will also implement it in the near future. The unification of the country is not far away. However, the people of our country are conservative and have deep-rooted habits that are difficult to change. In the course of promotion, resistance is often generated. Without widespread publicity, it is not enough to achieve the effect of being known to every household. Young students have not yet developed deep-rooted habits. If they can instill the content of the new metric system and the unified methods as early as possible, it will be of great benefit to the promotion of the metric system. For this reason, we have selectively copied the aforementioned laws and regulations, sent them for review, and hope that you will print and distribute them to the schools under your jurisdiction and the education bureaus of each county, set a date, and convene all students to explain the content of the new metric system and its promotion methods, in order to achieve the effect of taking the lead. As for the arithmetic textbooks used in primary and secondary schools, those that have incorporated the new metric system must be adopted as soon as possible to ensure consistency." In addition to replying to the letter, we are issuing the laws and regulations, ordering the schools to comply with the publicity, and the primary and secondary school arithmetic textbooks must adopt those that have incorporated the new metric system. This order.

The County Agricultural Education Center Organizes Winter Vacation Reading Groups for Farmers 154

The County Farmers' Education Center recognizes the importance of literacy for farmers and utilizes the winter slack season to organize winter vacation reading groups to seek educated farmers to guide the reading of useful books. The regulations for the regular reading groups are recorded as follows: (1) This association is named the regular reading group of the Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center in the first civil education district of Shanghai County. (2) The purpose of this association is to use agricultural leisure to increase reading interest and study applied academics. (3) Anyone near the center who has received considerable education and has been approved by the association can fill out an application form to become a member. (4) This association is divided into the following two groups: 1. Elementary school group: Anyone who has graduated from elementary school or has an elementary school education enters the elementary school group. 2. Middle school group: Anyone who has graduated from elementary school and received secondary education or above enters the middle school group. (5) This association has one director who manages the affairs of the association, and one secretary for each of the elementary school group and the middle school group, who is responsible for the affairs of their respective groups. (6) Members of this association must choose at least one type of book, and read it themselves after being approved by the director of the association. (7) Members of this association should write a reading report or a paper every three days. (8) Members of this association meet once every two days to discuss difficult problems, which are convened by the director. (9) This association may hire a number of volunteers to grade the results and provide guidance on research. (10) The excellent results of the members will be compiled and published. (11) The expenses of this association will be borne by the Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center. (12) This association is from January 22nd to the end of February, 22nd year. (13) These regulations will be implemented after being approved by the board of directors and submitted to the County Education Bureau for approval.

Educational Cooperation Between National Tongji University and Municipal Wusong Middle School 157

丨To be implemented from the next semester丨

▲Wusong Junior High Graduates Exempted from Entrance Exam to Tongji High School

National Tongji University, in view of the successful operation of Municipal Wusong Middle School, has decided to establish an educational cooperation agreement with the school starting from the next semester. The main points are: ㈠ All equipment, school grounds, and fields will be used jointly. ㈡ Wusong Middle School will add German classes, and students are free to enroll. Those who pass the examination and graduate can be admitted to Tongji High School without an entrance exam and will be exempted from the one-year preparatory class in German. Previously, Tongji University required ordinary junior high school graduates who wished to enter the university's high school to study German for one year upon admission. This agreement has been separately approved by the Ministry of Education and the Bureau of Education and will be implemented from the next semester.

The new Eastern District Elementary School built by the Public Works Department on Jingzhou Road will be completed and renovated on February 1st. The new building on Jingzhou Road, except for the kindergarten and first grade, will exclusively enroll male students. This proposal has now been approved and will be implemented this year. It is noted that the Public Works Department operates Chinese elementary schools in the Eastern District, including one on Huishan Road and one on Huade Road. During the last meeting of the Education Committee of the Public Works Department, the budget for Western children's schools for this year was discussed. Under the item of temporary construction expenses, it was proposed to allocate 160,000 taels to build a Western children's school in the Western District. This item has been marked as urgent. However, the exact amount will be subject to re-estimation by the Public Works Department or further reduction. It is also proposed to allocate 100,000 taels to cover part of the construction costs of the Hanbury Girls' School for Western children, which is also marked as urgent. The regular expenses of the Education Department (Western schools section) and various Western children's schools have also been reviewed, but may still be adjusted by the Finance Department. The architectural plan for the Hanbury Girls' School for Western children has been reviewed by the Architectural Subcommittee, which believes that some points should be redesigned, and the site should be closer to the northern boundary so that the sports field on the side facing the target range can be expanded. The above proposals have been approved by the Board of Directors.

Recent News from the White Goose Painting Tutorial School 161

The famous art group, the White Goose Grand Meeting, after actively reviving and announcing its establishment on New Year's Day, has been supplemented and approved for registration by the Municipal Bureau of Education, expanded its organization, and established the White Goose Painting Tutorial School to provide correct guidance and opportunities for those who seek self-improvement and have artistic talent. The facilities are striving for perfection, and the management is rigorous. The formal opening of the school is scheduled for mid-February. The class is divided into four day and night sessions. Many people are enthusiastically requesting prospectuses and registering. The winter vacation tutorial class is very short-term, and those who wish to join the painting tutorial must register as soon as possible.

Different Tactics, Each With Its Own Skill

Military Academy Basketball Team Loses to Soochow University 167

▲Soochow University Wins 63-46 After Initial Defeat

▲Military Academy Takes the Lead in the First Half, Loses After Key Player is Fouled Out

Military Academy's Bad Luck, Both Forwards Fouled Out

Military Academy to Play St. John's Tonight at 8 PM

The Nanjing Central Military Academy basketball team, invited to Shanghai, lost its first match against Soochow University last night, suffering a defeat of 63-46. In the first half, the Military Academy led 26-23 by three points. Although the Military Academy lost, its performance was excellent. The accuracy of its long-range shots was particularly commendable. In the second half, the two forwards, Liu Gongchang, were fouled out with four fouls each. Soochow University took the opportunity to launch a fierce attack, and the Military Academy eventually lost its defense. The audience regretted it, and it was attributed to bad luck. Tonight at 8 PM, they will play St. John's, still at the Western YMCA.

▲Strengths and Weaknesses of the Military Academy 168

▲Entirely Relies on Long-Range Shots The outstanding feature of the Military Academy is its accurate long-range shooting, especially Liu Gongchang. He rarely misses when he raises his hand to shoot from afar. The entire team's offensive method is to pass the ball forward with high passes, relying on their tall and strong physiques. When they reach outside the free-throw line, they shoot the ball into the basket, never attempting shots near the basket.

▲Poor Jump Balls by Center Center Huang Jianding did not show his strengths last night and was not outstanding. Losing the jump balls was a major cause of the defeat. Soochow University won every jump ball at opportune moments and scored by dribbling straight to the basket. The Military Academy lost more than just ten or twenty points because of this. The inability to shoot near the basket is also a weakness. Their straightforward, non-turning offensive method needs improvement.

▲Two Backs Are Commendable Their defensive strategy of using a five-man zone defense kept Soochow University at bay in the first half. However, it broke down in the second half. Captain Wang Shixuan was the most outstanding of the two backs, excelling in both offense and defense. He is the brain of the entire team. With Gao Lingzhao, both are tall and strong, making it difficult for Soochow University's attacks. Overall, the team is above average and not just an ordinary team.

▲Soochow University Wins After Initial Defeat

▲The Golden Age of the Military Academy In the first minute of the game, Soochow University won the jump ball twice in a row. Feng Nianhua turned around and broke into the basket to score. He repeated the move several times, taking a 4-0 lead. The Military Academy then strengthened its defense and tied the score at 4-4. They then took a 6-4 lead. Thanks to Liu Gongchang's beautiful long-range shots, they led the way, with Soochow University only able to follow. The Military Academy's peak was 20-11 and 26-15. Soochow University worked hard and added eight points. The Military Academy had the upper hand in the first half, winning by three points at 26-23.

▲Forwards are Fouled Out When the second half began, the Military Academy added two more points. However, Soochow University replaced Feng Nianhua, who had three fouls, with Yuan Qingwu, who broke through the Military Academy's defense. As expected, the score gradually became tied at 30. Then, the situation suddenly changed. Liu Gongchang, the Military Academy's best shooter, was fouled out with four fouls. Soochow University took the opportunity to launch a major offensive. Sure enough, they took a 36-34 lead by two points.

▲The Entire Situation Changes From then on, the Military Academy's offensive power greatly diminished. Soochow University's shots were extraordinary, and they won by ten points at 44-34. The Military Academy narrowed the gap to 46-40, still six points behind. Soochow University then scored several times in a row, reaching 54-44. Li Gongyu, the Military Academy's left forward, was also fouled out with four fouls. As a result, the entire team faltered and could not recover. At the end of the game, Soochow University won 63-46.

Spring and Autumn

Shanghai Gossip 172

— Zhongxian

▲Two Faces

Shanghai people's faces are like gold ingots, they have a "head," but flipping them over, there are only two faces: one true face, one false face. There's really nothing new.

Most Shanghai people, after nodding and smiling at someone, will open their mouths and ask, "Old Shi, have you eaten?" In fact, he doesn't need to know about other people's eating habits at all. Whether or not other people eat has nothing to do with him. It can be seen that he is being disingenuous from the start.

If you show your true face when dealing with the world, you will inevitably suffer losses and setbacks everywhere. Everyone has to use a false face to maneuver around everything, so the faces we see are all "reverse sides," and we never see the "front" of the face.

Shanghai people are like this, and Shanghai as a place is also like this.

How beautiful is the surface of Shanghai! Flat, wide roads, three-dimensional, magnificent buildings, electric lights shining like daylight, and other dedicated material civilization are unimaginable to people from the interior. Shanghai is truly like heaven!

What is the reverse side of Shanghai? This is not easily seen by people walking on the streets. Only a small fraction of it can be seen in newspaper reports.

Snow and Blood 173

— Yiyiguan Lord

丨Words Sound the Same Despite Being Different丨

Many days of warmth, one night of north wind, and then this heavy snow blew in.

Speaking of this "snow," from ancient times to the present, poets and writers have created so many anecdotes for it. What is it like to step on snow to find plum blossoms, what is it like to compose poems about snow, and what is it like to enjoy the snow scene with lamb wine? There are so many timely pleasures that cannot be said enough. In short, in the past, during times of "national peace and prosperity," this "snow" was the most beautiful decoration of the human world!

However, during this "national crisis," wherever the iron hooves of the tyrannical sun reached, the mountains and rivers of our country changed color. Only the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteers shed blood to resist the enemy! So, now, one night of north wind has blown in this heavy snow, just because this snow blown in by the north wind at this time, I feel a bit of the bloodiness of the volunteers. At the same time, I feel even more that this "snow" and "blood," although the words are different, sound the same. In the past, during times of "national peace and prosperity," this was naturally not felt. However, now, during the "period of national crisis," seeing this "snow" cannot help but make me think of that "blood" - the blood of the volunteers. I wonder if the people of our country, when seeing this pure white "snow" at this time, can think of that bright red "blood"?

Modern Trilogy 174

— Junshan

丨Movies, Dancing, Golf丨

"Miss ×, would you like to go to the movies? The film at the Cathay today is very good."

Such a request is certainly very polite to a girlfriend and can be considered elegant if you propose it to your girlfriend like that. But in fact, it is often not that easy. Being polite is of course another matter, because the answer often ends up being something like this: "Sorry, I already have an engagement," or "Oh, I'm not free. Mr. Zhang has asked me to go to the Camidrome to feather dance."

From the latter result, it tells you that going to the movies is certainly modern, that goes without saying, but isn't dancing also modern? So if you want to be completely modern, you must know how to dance. Of course, if you can invite someone to see a movie, you can certainly invite them to dance, but taking a step back, you have to dance to be considered modern, and there's no denying that.

× × ×

"Mr. Li, will we golf? Can you play?"

"The St. Anna Golf Course is considered the best, what do you think?"

"·········"

Such a question is often asked directly by your girlfriends, or in the movie theater, in the cafe, on the dance floor, or in other conversations.

"After this dance, shall we go and play Wee Golf? Mr. Zhang."

"Boy, buy two golf tickets."

"·········"

Similar conversations are often used by modern young men to woo their girlfriends.

× × ×

Therefore, to meet the requirements of this modern era, you must be familiar with this trilogy: movies, dancing, and golf.

Inside, the skills of opening doors, whirlwinds, robbers, or racketeers. So I have to persuade everyone again that, when you are well-fed and have a life of wine and lights, it is best to think of a way to settle these poor friends. At the very least, you must not be stingy when it comes to giving rice or clothing. At the same time, the police force must also increase positions and patrol day and night. If they see that someone is giving alms and that there is strict prevention, they will not dare to break the law.

The Effect of Birth Control 175

— Yi'an

丨Two Points Worth Noting丨

This is the opinion of an expert; nowadays, many people in civilized societies, especially women, are advocating birth control, believing that a better selection of the human race can be achieved, that the poor can reduce their burden, that women in the working class can reduce the care of their children, and that women can reduce the pain of pregnancy and childbirth. Apart from the third and fourth points being factual, the other two points are quite noteworthy. Facts tell us that the result of birth control is that the birth rate of the excellent class decreases much more, while the birth rate of the non-excellent class increases relatively. Because those who know how to use birth control methods mostly belong to the excellent class, and their methods and prevention are relatively more thorough. Therefore, the birth rate of the excellent class will decrease sharply, while the birth rate of the non-excellent class will increase relatively. So, will the society and human race of the future be relatively better?

A Guilty Conscience 176

— By Hongshou Du Juan

They anxiously helped him home, but Dongfang Sheng was already unconscious. By evening, he was somewhat lucid, and he raised his listless eyes, saying haltingly to the two of them, "…Being able to explain myself to my master by the pond could be considered fulfilling my long-held wish. After I die, please bury me by the Qiantang River, as I consider that the most suitable place for my final resting place. You two, I also know that you love each other, so please continue to love each other forever."

Xiaoman, upon hearing this, could only silently acknowledge it. She had no way, in this critical moment, to use the most appropriate and concise words to dispel the misunderstanding. Ouyang could only remain silent as well, his heart in a sea of remorse, knowing that this sin was entirely of his own making. Had he not shown his love for Xiaoman, he would never have caused the relapse of his close friend Dongfang Sheng's old ailment. Such a scar was truly etched too deeply into Ouyang's heart, and he would feel guilty for the rest of his life.

Dongfang's wife buried Dongfang Sheng by the Qiantang River. Nearby, there was a hospital founded by a Christian mission. She sold the villa and, with the maid, built another house next to the tomb. Apart from serving at the hospital during the day, she spent her mornings and evenings in the house by the tomb, hoping to atone for her life in this way.

After Dongfang Sheng's death, Ouyang Sheng continued his wandering life. He felt that his former family had not suffered enough. The guilt he felt for the sin he had committed against Dongfang Sheng caused him great mental anguish. Every time he recalled it, he was filled with boundless sorrow. Over the past five years, he had visited Dongfang's grave once a year to pay his respects. This time, he again walked involuntarily down this road. The road had only two rows of trees, just as it had in the past. He walked to the pond and found it even more desolate than before. Everything around him seemed to be angry at him, but he was willing to endure all the ridicule because his sin was too great.

× × × × × ×

Ouyang Sheng leaned against a tree, lost in thought, the entire history of his sin flashing before him, scene by scene, up to his current visit to the pond. He suddenly felt a slight evening breeze, which was quite chilly. The sky was gradually turning white, clearly already dawning. He did not know why he had been lost in thought all night. He walked back the way he had come, the trees on both sides nodding as if to see him off, perhaps saying, "Mr. Ouyang, you don't need to feel guilty. Strive for your future and repay your friend!" (The End)

The Art of Night Walking 177

— By Long

丨Thinking of Ways for Poor Friends丨

The sharp, scissor-like north wind is attacking people again. Aside from adding layers of heavy clothing, people have practically no other way to defend themselves.

Does this mean that the propertied class has nothing to fear? No, no, no. The starving and freezing demons are calculating their winter food and clothing needs and intend to resolve them by falling on you. The heavier your leather coat, the greater their benefit.

Wherever the streetlights are dim, the place is desolate and deserted, and beyond the gaze of the police, is their sphere of influence. In the dead of night, when the wind howls like waves and the shadows of trees resemble ghosts, that is when their sentries are densely deployed, choosing people to devour. If you are careless and breach the defense line, they will treat you as a pig breaking out of its pen, brandishing their knives and proceeding directly to skin you alive. Even if the victim does not lose their life, they will surely fall ill from the cold. Therefore, I advise you all, in the winter nights, to go home early if you are out and about, and to go to bed early if you are at home, to avoid unexpected losses and frights. But then again, their food and clothing problems still need to be resolved. If they gain nothing at night, it may become a problem during the day. Nowadays, most of those who practice birth control belong to the middle and upper classes. As for the lower classes, they continue to live as usual, so their burden has not been reduced. As things stand in America, all male students who are minors and older female students in higher education have learned methods of birth control. Because more young people have learned birth control methods, sexual morality is deteriorating day by day.

Art Publication

A Record of Exploring Yinan (Part Two) 178

— By Zhu Hairen

丨Entering the Geng Cave丨

Tea and snacks were served. Relying on electric torches, we were guided by Elder Chu and Director Mao, touring the various small caves on both sides. Such as the Water Curtain, the Underground Passage, the Elephant's Trunk, the Snoring Nose, and the Seven Stars, etc. The stone steps spiraled, sometimes ascending and sometimes descending. Some were deeply secluded, and the cold air pierced the skin; others had faint sunlight filtering through, as if traveling underground. Inside the caves were stone tables, stone beds, and stone benches. Two stone pillars stood upright, piercing the sky, like central river pillars. Beside the pillars was a pool of clear water, said to be piously obtained by Elder Chu, and all the cave's drinking water was taken from here. There was also a huge rock towering like a giant dragon opening its mouth, with two stones below resembling fish, one facing in and one facing out. They were appropriately named "Carp Leaping Over the Dragon Gate," truly fitting. The small caves were all secluded and tightly winding, low and narrow. Emerging from one and entering another was like a butterfly flitting through flowers, almost as if one's body had transformed into a microbe traveling through blood vessels. The stone steps in the cave numbered over a thousand, proving the scale of the construction. Elder Chu had been managing these two caves for over ten years, spending nearly 200,000 yuan, almost exhausting his fortune. Ms. Manhua also provided assistance, and her enthusiasm and determination are commendable. Alas, Elder Chu is an extraordinary man! If he could use his talents to rescue the people from fire and water, why is he so infatuated with these two caves? Could it be that his mischievous heart is still not satisfied, and the phoenix and dragon must hide their might? From this, a gentleman can observe the changes in the world. However, where there are outstanding people, there is blessed land. The two caves are even more famous thanks to Elder Chu's name, and in the years to come, anyone who passes by will surely linger and be reluctant to leave. Thus, Elder Chu's contribution will be immortal.

I, together with the brothers Boxiang and Bozhou, toured together, not leaving each other's side. We both sought out the hidden and explored the secluded, and took photographs to leave our footprints. In a few short hours, our heels never stopped, and not only did we not feel tired, but we lamented the shortness of time. How great is the power of the scenery to move people! Boxiang even wanted to examine its features more closely, to prepare for his future paintings, and his toil must have been even greater than mine.

After the tour, we climbed back to the rear cave to watch Ms. Nengzi perform sword dancing: dressed in tight-fitting clothes with narrow sleeves, she possessed ample grace. The double swords swirled, their silver light shimmering, followed by double knives, achieving the utmost in swift and agile movements. Ms. Nengzi is skilled in poetry and calligraphy and is also familiar with music, so swordplay is merely an additional skill. After the dance, Elder Chu requested calligraphy and painting as a token of appreciation. I am ashamed of my lack of talent and unable to fulfill the request, which is regrettable. As we were leaving, Elder Chu ordered firecrackers to be lit to see us off. His deep friendship and high regard left those who experienced it at a loss for how to repay him. The lingering beauty of the place made it unbearable to leave indifferently.

After leaving the cave, we walked back to the boat. Mr. Hu Boxiang, an old friend of Elder Chu, discussed the aesthetic construction of the cave with him along the way, tirelessly. At nine o'clock, we had dinner. During the meal, Elder Chu described the historical traces of the cave in detail, like reading a record of searching for spirits in a thousand treasures, making people happy and forgetful of fatigue. He also said that once the cave affairs were completed, he would retreat from the mundane world, to leave the secular world. Elder Chu has been cultivating his nature and seeking truth for twenty years, and has faintly realized the origin, liberated the six senses, and driven the old cart out of the burning house, which is in agreement with his inner thoughts. Someone like me, without learning, how can I glimpse even a ten-thousandth of his understanding? What a pity that in such a hasty meeting, I encountered a good teacher but could not ask for more advice, which I regret.

On the morning of the 27th, we left Yi and arrived in Xi in the afternoon, taking the Shanghai-Nanjing train back to Shen. During this trip, Elder Chu and his nephew, as well as his daughter Ms. Nengzi, and daughter-in-law Ms. Manhua, all entertained us warmly, which was especially touching. Director Mao took time out of his busy schedule to guide us, accompanying us along the way. The boat trip was dull, but he made us laugh and relieved our boredom, doing everything he could to entertain us. Without Mr. Mao, how could we have felt so at home? So Mr. Ao's contribution was not small. As for the transportation, accommodation, and meals along the way, they were all properly taken care of by the standing committee members of the group, Yao Yuangan and Liu Yuqi, whose enthusiasm is truly admirable. I include this to express my sincere gratitude.

With the settlement period approaching and cotton yarn trading suspended for a week, unpredictable foreign cotton movements are causing more liquidations and increased downward pressure. However, buyers are holding firm due to low inventory levels. Nevertheless, 8,000 bales of coarse Tianjin cotton arrived at the docks yesterday (mostly handled by the Shenxin factory). Considering the current situation, the market is unlikely to break out of its current range-bound pattern in the short term.

Sluggish Zheng Standard The Zheng Standard market opened with the lingering effects of the previous day's weakness. Market sentiment remained weak, with fewer buyers. Prices for all months fell by 0.05 to 0.015 taels. The second session in the afternoon also declined, with a slight rise at the close. Ultimately, prices for all months fell by 0.05 to 0.01 taels. Total daily trading volume was 21,400 dan. Geng Feng sold 2,900 dan, Zhang Da 1,100 dan, Ming De 1,000 dan, Yi Yu 2,100 dan, and He Shen 900 dan. Ming Hua bought 1,400 dan, Da Chang 800 dan, and Chang Feng 1,800 dan. Closing prices were as follows:

Zheng Standard Gains, Losses, Balances: May 342.0, down 1.5, 60,600

February 331.5, down 2.5, 144,900 June 344.0, down 1.0, 25,600

March 337.0, down 2.0, 115,100 Total 443,900

April 339.5, down 1.5, 97,700

Stagnant Actual Demand Spot cotton demand has ceased, with factories not processing. Falling cotton futures are further reducing trading volume. The source of supply is estimated at 300 bales of Tonghua cotton.

World Cotton Market Mixed 188

Yesterday, due to a lack of sellers, strong Wall Street activity spurred reactionary buying in American cotton. The market was quiet but firm, with futures rising 2 to 6 points and spot prices rising 5 points. British cotton futures rose 3-4 points, while spot prices fell 3 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell 3 points. Indian cotton was mediocre, with Pingguoer falling 0.25 rupees, Bairoxi falling 1.25 rupees, and Aomula falling 1.5 rupees. Rice Market Dull Amidst War Rumors 190

▲Only a Few Transactions... Business Depends on Rising Prices▲

▲Yesterday, over 30 boats arrived at the South Market, with scattered transactions and lackluster sales due to the approaching end of the year. Although over 1,000 shi of bundled rice arrived, it could not reverse the declining trend, and prices continued to fall by 3-4 jiao. However, the supply of Qingjiao thin rice was limited, allowing it to maintain its price. Su Tong, Chang, and Nangang rice prices slightly decreased by 3-4 jiao, and Bianyuan rice was unavailable. Yinyuan softened. Only one boat of Qingjiao Duzi arrived in the entire market, commanding a premium due to its scarcity, with prices ranging from 10 yuan to 9.9 yuan.

▲Over 10 boats arrived at the North Market yesterday, but sales were extremely sluggish. Merchants were eager to close their books, causing prices to drop by another 3-4 jiao. Gaobaijing rice from the North decreased by more than 1 jiao, with medium and lower grades decreasing by 3-4 jiao. Early rice and thin rice also fell by 2 jiao. Yangxian and Yinyuan rice were generally weak. Baiyuan Dujian was stable, while Buxian and Kexian were fixed.

▲Kexian rice was even more sluggish. Although there were over 40,000 bags in the market, some were purchased by speculators hoping for higher prices next year, while others were owned by Hunan and Jiangxi customers and merchants who also planned to hold out until prices rose. While Kexian merchants were willing to buy, it was difficult to obtain supplies. Only a few small traders, due to their limited capital, were selling as soon as they received goods. However, Kexian sales were mainly limited to Fujian province, which still had some demand, but most merchants had also closed their books, waiting for higher prices. With both buyers and sellers lacking enthusiasm, the market was particularly quiet. Yesterday, only the local street merchants sold 397 bags of Hunan machine oil rice. There were no transactions by Fujian merchants. The price was 9.19 yuan, a slight improvement of 0.02 yuan compared to the previous day. However, most sellers were determined to hold out until after the new year, expecting high oil rice to reach over 9.5 yuan.

Flour Market Unstable After Brief Rally 192

Foreign Wheat Prices Remain Low... Actual Sales Merchants Gradually Selling Off

After the flour market opened yesterday morning, prices for all months appeared stable, as foreign wheat prices rebounded by 0.02 to 0.04 yuan. Initial market sentiment was slightly boosted, about 0.0075 yuan better than the previous day's closing price. However, after the second session, prices gradually softened as actual sales merchants slightly sold off their positions, causing the market to decline again. When the afternoon session opened, prices for both near and distant months were unstable, as current foreign wheat prices remained low. Australian wheat was quoted at 3.6 taels, and Canadian No. 3 wheat was quoted at 3.56 taels. This situation severely dampened the enthusiasm of speculators. Moreover, actual sales merchants continued to sell off their positions, suggesting limited prospects. Although Henan merchants were buying, their actions were ignored, leading to a general decline in the market. Ultimately, the current month was down 0.0075 yuan, February was down 0.0075 yuan, March was down 0.005 yuan, April was down 0.0125 yuan, May was down 0.0075 yuan, and June was down 0.005 yuan.

Rumors of Modifications to Woolen Fabric Import Tariffs

▲Rising Wool Prices Expected to Increase Pricing

Woolen Fabric Wholesale Transactions Have Halted Due to Busy Payments... Information for Reference is Listed Below

(1) Over 500 bales of Walter tweed, floral tweed, and horse tweed are being shipped from London to Shanghai and are expected to arrive soon.

(2) Sichuan merchants stationed in Shanghai are inquiring about market prices and will likely purchase after funds arrive.

(3) Foreign firms have recently received telegrams from foreign mills indicating that wool prices have increased, leading to significant price increases for woolen fabrics.

(4) It is widely rumored among industry members that tariff regulations on woolen fabrics will be revised in June or July of this year.
