Free Talk

Madman (3) 205

— Ling He

At this time, everyone was paying attention to the dog and its puppies, so they didn't pay much attention to the madman. Unexpectedly, the madman picked up a large stone and aimed it at the dog, hitting it on the head. At that moment, the women all cried out, and the children ran out from the crowd. The dog, which was in labor, struggled for a few moments before becoming completely still. However, the puppies that had already been born did not seem to feel any sadness and were still moving in their mother's embrace, hoping to suck a few drops of milk from her slightly warm breast. But the mother was already dead.

No one knew when, but the madman had already left. All that remained were the mother dog and several other women. The two lepers were also staring blankly at the dead dog, muttering softly,

"Damn madman!"

But the dog was dead, and that was that. The puppies would soon die too. Although this might tug at people's heartstrings, it would only be for a moment. The women soon began talking about the madman again.

They talked for a long time. The two lepers were now listening to the dog's owner saying:

"But Wang Lao Si was a rather ambitious person, and he spoke very rationally. When he had nothing to do in the evenings, he would sit at my door and chat. He often said: 'I'm getting older every day, and I still don't have a wife. If this continues, won't my line be cut off? But after all these years of hardship, I've finally found someone. If the ancestors protect me, and I can marry her and have a son or daughter, I'll die content.'

"So, he made up his mind to take advantage of this year's good harvest. If the gods bless us with a good yield, he would sell the excess next month and buy a new quilt so that his wife would have a clean bed when she came. But then he discussed with me:

'I still owe Uncle Wu's family several loads of old rent. Should I pay it back or not? His family's accountant has already come to urge me several times.'

'Just owe it for another year,' I said. 'Go to Uncle Wu and plead with him nicely. He's been an official and is literate and reasonable. Besides, Auntie Wu is a kind person who prays and does good deeds. She'll probably take pity on you.'

"I said this to him, and he thought it made sense. ... Who knew that someone so sensible would suddenly go mad? Heaven really has no eyes!"

Everyone listened in silence, not knowing what to say. Then the dog's owner seemed to want to say something more, her lips moving, so the two lepers quickly chimed in:

"Wu Lao Si was fine when he went to my master's house to pay the rent the day before yesterday."

Perhaps this sentence was not loud enough to attract much attention. At this time, someone else was talking about how the government soldiers had raped Wang Lao Si's wife years ago, and how his wife had been so chaste that she refused to submit, and was eventually killed in a flurry of knives. But because the people there didn't pay attention to him, the two lepers angrily ran away. (End)

"Don't Move" vs. "Must Move" 206

— Yang Xingzhi

On December 7th of the year before last, Mr. Dai Jitao published an "Open Letter to Educators and Parents of Students Throughout the Country." The most alarming sentences in the letter were: "Saplings cannot grow if they are free; young people cannot become adults if they are free." Recently, Mr. Zhou Fohai, the Director of Education of Jiangsu Province, also published a "Letter to Parents of Students Throughout Jiangsu," which contains many thought-provoking remarks, such as: "Resisting teachers and violating discipline, taking rebellion as the spirit of revolution, acting recklessly and wantonly, taking arbitrariness as the development of personality... As a result, there are trends of expelling leaders and choosing teachers in schools, and claims of non-filial revolution at home." The arguments in Dai's and Zhou's letters are exactly the same, and Zhou's writing is actually better and more appealing than Dai's in terms of vigor and sharpness. I think that "old people" will definitely toast to it, while "young people" will definitely stick out their tongues after reading it.

From Dai's letter to Zhou's letter, we can clearly see the current government's demands on the people. The true meaning of this demand is "internal stability," and "rectifying academic conduct" and "〇〇" are actually two sides of the same coin.

Originally, since the September 18th Incident the year before last, not only young people, but almost everyone has been "moving" and "changing." The entire society has been turbulent in the waves of unrest. However, this turbulent situation is not accidental; it is the result of the combined pressure of foreign aggression and internal strife, and also the trend of a turning point in the times.

"Stillness!" "Stability!" "No freedom allowed!" "Those who are free!" These are the calls of Mr. Dai and Mr. Zhou, and also the calls of the government. However, from the perspective of thousands of years of history, both in China and abroad, people will never give up freedom, and the times have never accepted the order to "turn back." If you don't allow movement, what if the times insist on moving?

In the Tram 207

— Zheng Boqi

A Sketch of Shanghai Petty Bourgeois Life

The tram is about to leave. A jumps on the car lightly, pushes open the door, and sees B at a glance.

B, A (almost at the same time): Ah! Haven't seen you in a long time! Haven't seen you in a long time! Where are you going?

A (sitting next to B): I'm going to ×× Bridge. And you?

B: I'm just going up ahead. Haven't seen you in a long time!

A: Haven't seen you in a long time! How's business?

B: So-so. The market's too sluggish now. Are you doing well?

A: Just muddling through. Business is very difficult now!

B: Come visit me when you're free.

A: Okay. Please come over when you're free too. I have a lot of good friends there.

B: (At this time, A buys a ticket) What's your phone number there?

A: We just moved, and the phone hasn't been installed yet.

B: It's annoying to install a phone now! It takes at least half a year.

A: We have connections, and it'll be installed soon.

B: My phone number is 43675! Call me first when you want to come.

A (takes out a notebook): Please write it down there. Ah! I'm sorry! What's your surname? I forgot.

B (writing at once): Yes, yes. I'll write it all down for you.

A (looking at the notebook): Yes. Mr. Wang, I'm so stupid! Didn't we meet at the dog track last time?

B: You were with your wife.

A: That's right, that's right. She lost terribly that day, it was so funny.

B: What kind of business are you doing this year?

A: This year, I'm only buying and not selling. I buy whatever's cheap. If iron is cheap, I buy iron; if piece goods fall, I buy piece goods. I don't even use cash for the transactions, I just buy it first. Then I'll sell it when the price goes up. This way of doing things is still good.

B: That's one way to do it.

A: It's always better to work for yourself than to help others. In this day and age, it's good enough just to muddle through.

B: In this day and age, who isn't just muddling through? Doing it your way, you can save on expenses.

A: Sigh! Don't even mention expenses. I have two families, and each one needs 300 yuan a month, so that's 600 yuan in total. And neither one is willing to take less. All year long, I'm busy, but I'm just busy supporting my families.

B: Isn't that the truth? It's not easy to support even one family, let alone two.

A: What can I do! When I first came out of school, I was in a foreign firm, earning less than twenty yuan a month, and still had to save ten or so. Now I earn more, but it's still never enough to cover expenses.

B: Alas! We're all in the same boat. Ah, I've arrived, I need to get off. Come over and visit when you're free.

B gets off the car hurriedly. A leans against the carriage wall, looks out the window, and whistles the tune "Love Me Tonight."

Ticket seller (walking up to A): Sir, you've gone past your stop, please pay an extra fare.

A: What! Have I arrived already? How much do I need to add?

Ticket seller: Where are you going, exactly?

A: I'm going to ×× Bridge.

Ticket seller: Please add a short-distance ticket, seven cents.

A: Okay. It's only half a stop. I'll get off now.

Ticket seller: I can't let you off without paying, I'll get punished.

A (angry): Why didn't you tell me earlier? I refuse to pay! Are you the only ones allowed to cheat? (Suddenly softening) Let's just call it even.

The car has arrived at ×× Bridge. A jumps off.

Ticket seller: Cheat? Have I ever cheated you? (To the outside of the window) Wearing such nice Western clothes, but all you know how to do is cheat, damn it...!

Snowy Morning 208

— Zhou Lengjia

Snowflakes are falling.

The sky is like a giant winnowing fan, scattering flour. The ground, the walls, the roofs, are all white, the accumulated powder is an inch thick.

Opening the door, a gust of cold wind hits the face, causing a sharp pain. Snowflakes cover the body, like cotton wadding.

Holding an umbrella, walking on the road, the snow has been trampled into mud, making it slippery.

The roadside trees, French plane trees, have shed all their leaves, leaving only bare branches reaching towards the sky, snow pressing on the bare branches, desolate.

The street cleaner, holding a long-handled broom, bends over to sweep the snow. Hot air comes out of his mouth and nose, like two streaks of white smoke.

A foreign lady, in a thick fur coat, high heels, walks across the road with a clatter, leading a Pekingese dog, its mouth gnawing on a piece of raw beef, a brass bell under its neck jingles and jangles.

The dog, of course, is luckier than the street cleaner.

On Hualong Road, under a large umbrella, several coolies squeeze together, warmly enjoying their breakfast—"Lao Doufu Jiang, how many coppers for a bowl?"

A maid puts a copper kettle on the stove, turns around and warms her hands. The back of her hand is swollen like bread, her fingers swollen like red carrots.

"Beep beep beep!" A car rushes through the snow and mud, flying forward. Inside the car, a trendy couple sits closely together, their hearts and dreams in the thirty-third heaven.

Xiafei Road is like falling into an ice pot, not even half a ghost. Only two or three White Russians, shivering, huddle in the alleyway.

Snowflakes are falling, like the sky shaking a winnowing fan and scattering flour.

The air is fifteen degrees below zero.

Not even a beggar can be seen, tomorrow the newspapers will definitely report several frozen corpses.

The snowy French Concession, how cold! How quiet!

Snow Night March 209

—

In the dark night, I walk forward on the snowy ground!

Snow, icy snow, keeps drifting onto my head, hitting my body, hitting my face, cold, cold. Wind, piercing wind, keeps roaring in my ears, scraping against my body, scraping against my face, cold, cold.

However, I must move forward, I will never rest, and besides, where can I rest?

On the road, all I see is a silver glow, reflecting the desolate streetlights, a dim yellow. However, I do not feel fear, nor do I feel desolate, I only advance towards the future, who cares about it, that expanse, white and boundless, white and boundless.

Occasionally, I think of my hometown. Oh! Hometown, it's like this too, no lights, no moon, also such goose feather snow, white and boundless. My brothers are buried in the snowdrifts, my sisters die in the freezing cold. Cold, cold ah, I tremble, I am distressed... But not far away, I glimpse a fire, yo! That fire, is my hope, so I still move forward, I do not lose heart.

The wind blows hard, the snow flies densely, advance, advance,

In the distance, a few rooster crows tell me that the night is deep, and the cold has congealed. Here, darkness is approaching light, advance, advance, advance!

Oh! I advance, I dare not rest, and besides, where can I rest?

A Long Creation

The Crossroads of Era and Love (Continued) 210

— Zhang Ziping

She was really wiping her tears. Where did such cheap tears come from? She wasn't a movie star; she couldn't just cry whenever she wanted.

"Mrs. Zeng!..."

"........................................"

But she just held a snow-white handkerchief to rub her eyes, ignoring him. He knew that she was clearly changing her battle plan because her offensive had failed, switching from offense to defense.

"She's taking a defensive stance. What should I do? Take the offensive? That wouldn't be appropriate! She has reinforcements. If I take the offensive, I'll definitely be completely defeated. I still have to take a defensive stance, and not just a defensive stance, but also non-resistance!..."

He pondered for a while. In the end, he still couldn't restrain himself.

"Mrs. Zeng, why bother?"

He reached out his right hand and gently patted her shoulder.

"I'm not happy!"

She shrugged her shoulders slightly.

"I'm not angry. But I have my own worries..."

"You're angry! You're angry at me! You're clearly angry at me!"

"If you want to say that, what can I do?"

"You have to promise me that you won't be angry like that again. You have no idea how heartbroken I am when I see you angry, Mr. Lin!"

"Okay, okay. I won't be angry again."

"Then I'll be happy."

She smiled again.

He thought, if he was determined to love her, he should take this opportunity to show her his feelings, and he would definitely gain her sympathy. Otherwise, it could be said that she was clearly hinting at pursuing his sympathy.

Keeping Up Appearances Is Important 211

— Shi Gong

So poor that they can't pay the rent, with no rice for dinner, they secretly pawn their quilts and cotton robes. Yet, the old madam, the eldest daughter, the carriage driver, the servants—all the trappings of prosperous times—are still indispensable. When a party invitation arrives, even if it's guaranteed to lose money, they have to make a trip to the Little Garden. Even though their pockets are full of pawn tickets, they can't refuse to sit down and pretend, claiming a headache. This is supposedly called "keeping up appearances." As a Shanghainese who can't even dream of being a real person, if you don't grit your teeth and do this, you'll lose face and bring shame to your ancestors for generations.

The imperialists, clearly wanting to maintain and expand all their legal and illegal rights, desperately woo the aggressors and oppress the invaded. Yet, they insist on painting their faces red and white, twisting and turning as they sing a few lines about "morality" and "justice," dangling the bait in front of the invaded. Today, a telegram says Country A favors Country B; tomorrow, a dispatch says Country A suppresses Country B. They keep holding meaningless meetings, while the actual problems are left to the Four Heavenly Kings riding the clouds, suspended eight feet in the air. In reality, the so-called favoring or suppressing is just a show. To put it bluntly, imperialists always help imperialists. Don't expect them to help weak nations. But why do imperialists put on such airs? Supposedly, this is also called "keeping up appearances." If they didn't act soft and hard, hard and soft, this large imperialist group would lose its prestige and never be able to reopen the old shop.

Indeed, from individuals to international relations, everyone sees "face" as the number one key to self-cultivation, family management, national governance, and world peace. "A scholar will not bend his waist for five pecks of rice," "Starving to death is a small matter, losing integrity is a big deal"... the spirit of "face" is vividly on display. In reality, this situation is perfectly described by a saying from Pudong: "Putting a golden flower on a mangy head, bearing the pain to look good." Pudong people also have another saying that is very relevant to the way people live: "With an old face, the belly is full." People who worship hypocrisy will definitely scold this saying as "shameless." In fact, "poverty cannot be hidden, ugliness cannot be hidden." Why bother desperately "putting a golden flower on a mangy head"? That is truly "dying for face and suffering in life!"

Common Knowledge

Skin Diseases 212

— Sheng Yi

Skin diseases are the most common ailments we humans suffer from. Even if we don't have other illnesses, almost seventy to eighty percent of us have skin diseases. Now, I will describe the most common skin diseases in detail...

The most common skin diseases are roughly six types: ringworm, moles, spots, blisters, miliaria, and calluses. (1) Ringworm: There are two types of ringworm, scabies and favus, which are the most serious. Scabies, also known as scabies, is caused by a type of scabies mite that lives on the skin. Small blisters appear where the mites live, causing intense itching. People often scratch, and after scratching, scabs form, which is called dry scabies. If it becomes infected with pus, it is called wet scabies. It is very easy to transmit to people who sleep together. The treatment is to use sulfur, alcohol, talc, soap, lard, etc. to make an ointment, and apply it once a day until it is cured. Favus, also known as tinea capitis, is caused by a type of favus fungus that lives on the head. The area where the fungus lives first develops small, circular spots, then small blisters, and then forms small, yellow plates that emit a foul odor, causing hair to fall out and intense itching. People often scratch, even until it bleeds. The treatment is to first shave the hair, apply oil to the yellow plates to soften them, then peel them off, and then apply mercuric chloride and alcohol, and the disease will heal. (2) Moles: There are three types of moles: flesh moles, cinnabar moles, and blue moles. Flesh moles are raised on the skin, have no special color, and vary in shape and size. This is due to the development of dermal papillae. They can be cut off with a knife and then coated with an antiseptic, and they will heal. Cinnabar moles and blue moles are slightly raised compared to the skin and are mostly round. They are caused by the protrusion of the dermal papillae under the skin, as well as the deposition of pigment; red ones are called cinnabar moles, and blue ones are called blue moles. These moles are not harmful to the skin, but if you want to remove them, you can mix nitric acid or lime with blister beetle and apply it to the mole. After a few days, the mole will fall off. (3) Spots: There are three types of spots: birthmarks, freckles, and white spots. Birthmarks are present when a child is born. Red ones are called cinnabar birthmarks, and blue ones are called blue birthmarks. The size varies, and they do not protrude from the skin. Freckles are mostly black and often appear on the face. The size and number also vary, and they do not protrude from the skin. These two types of spots gradually develop due to the proliferation of pigment. White spots are white in color. The reason is the opposite of birthmarks and freckles. Instead, the pigment in the spotted area atrophies. They usually occur between the ages of ten and thirty, and the size varies. There are also cases where the entire body is white after birth, which is also a variation of white spots. (4) Acne: Acne often appears on the face and is caused by the accumulation of sebum in the sebaceous glands, but there is often a type of hair follicle mite that lives there at the same time. It usually occurs during adolescence. If it doesn't ulcerate, it is called acne, or comedones. If it ulcerates, it is called pustules. The treatment is to break it open with a needle and squeeze out the contents |pus and blood|, and then apply an antiseptic to heal. (5) Miliaria, also known as heat rash, is caused by the skin being soaked in sweat in hot weather, resulting in small red bumps that are constantly itchy. The treatment is to wash frequently when sweating a lot, and after washing, apply alcohol or floral water, and then use a powder that easily absorbs moisture to dust on the skin, and it will heal. (6) Calluses are hard skin that grows on the palms or soles of the feet, caused by the friction between the hands and feet and hard objects. Although they can be cut off with a knife, they will soon grow back. There is no way to cure them. There are also people who like to wear tight shoes, which causes hard skin to develop on the toes, causing pain when walking, which is called a corn. It is similar to a callus, but it has a central depression, which can be distinguished slightly. The treatment is to cut it off with a knife, or use medicine to soften it, but you must not wear tight shoes again in the future, and this will heal on its own, otherwise it will be ineffective.

The gentle east wind whispers its urging, from now on flying catkins are stained with mud, under the Stone City on the banks of the Shen River,

Raising Girls to Save the Nation 214

— Yi Ping

Getting off the tram, I have to turn into a long and dark alley to get to my house. Because I've walked it so many nights, I know how many steps it takes to reach the telephone pole sticking out in the middle of the road; where the puddles form after rain.

Last night, getting off the tram and turning into the alley entrance, I saw a crowd of people gathered around the trash can in the distance, each holding a kerosene lamp in their hand. This place, I never see people or lights when I return. "I wonder what happened?" I quickly walked a few steps, wondering.

"They're weighing it to play the lottery," said a worker-looking man cheerfully:

Hearing this, I had already guessed half of it in my heart. I walked closer to the trash can and looked behind the crowd, and sure enough, it was a dead child. "It's a boy" said the Suzhou amah sadly: but most of them agreed with the worker's proposal, preparing to make a fortune.

I left this group of people, avoided the telephone pole, jumped over the puddle, opened the back door, and groped my way into my bedroom in the dark. I sat down on the nearest chair, thinking, aimlessly thinking, forgetting to turn on the light.

This is not the first time I've encountered such a thing. Is it the child of a poor family? Impossible! No matter how poor the family is, and no matter how many children there are; even if they are born, the parents cannot raise them. But are there such cruel parents in the world who throw their own flesh and blood next to the trash can? They wouldn't give it to childless people, or send it to a charity. Say the child died as soon as it was born, that's also impossible. They would definitely cover it with something, or bury it in the wilderness. Originally, "death" is what people fear the most, and our country also has the saying, "entering the soil is peace", how can one throw away an innocent newborn child randomly? So I was sure it was an illegitimate child.

Thinking of illegitimate children, "illegitimate children" themselves are innocent, and the guilt should be attributed to their parents. But why does society arbitrarily harm illegitimate children? Is it the people who create the crime who are to blame, or is the fate of illegitimate children like this?

"Freedom of love", even country girls now know. China is like a small colt that hasn't learned to walk yet. Suddenly, a whip is lashed on its butt, so it strives, or rather, desperately runs forward randomly. As a result, under the name of "freedom of love", a great sin is created.

The city, especially, is a den of iniquity, all kinds of temptations and threats surrounding young people. University students talk about love, carriage drivers talk about love, the daughters of landlords talk about love, boatmen talk about love. The grand culmination of love is the illegitimate child thrown by the trash can.

The map of Guanwai has changed color. People who are drunk with freedom of love, create your illegitimate children! Perhaps in the future, even more names like "raising girls to save the nation" will be discovered.

Clerk Communications

Hesitation About Marrying a Prostitute 215

Dear Editor:

When I was fourteen years old, I dropped out of school due to poverty at home. I didn't get a job at the Shanghai × Money House until I was sixteen, after many requests. Unfortunately, last October, I was subjected to various stimuli. As someone with a weak will, I had the ill-conceived idea of seeking comfort in a drinking woman. Later, I met the prostitute Su Zhen, who knew that she would never have hope of getting ahead in this lowly profession. For the sake of her life, she gently followed me. Because I knew she was capable and knew what suffering was, I swore never to betray her, and we became confidants. It has been three months since we agreed on a lifelong alliance. But in my mind, there are always a few questions | (1) This matter has not been agreed to by my parents. If it is discovered that she is a prostitute, then it will definitely be strongly opposed. (2) Marriage must have a public ceremony; marrying a prostitute, I fear that I will be despised by relatives and friends, or it will affect my position. (3) She has been engaged in this lowly profession for four years. Will there be any harm to future fertility? (4) She is already twenty-three this year, but I am only nineteen years old. With such a difference in age, will there be physiological problems? (5) My financial ability is not yet able to bear the cost of marriage. She is willing to continue this life for one year, so that she can save some money. Will this plan work? (6) If I intend to break up with her, then we have deep affection for each other. How can the scars on our souls be erased? | Therefore, I hesitate to decide. I hope you can teach me. I respectfully wish you

Good health, Hong Yong, respectfully.

Editor's note; Prostitutes are generally considered to be the most lowly: indeed, they can not only make young people who go to pleasure-seeking degenerate; even they themselves have the danger of "being like entering a stall selling spoiled fish, and not smelling the stench for a long time." But this cannot be generalized. There are also not a few who are capable and know what suffering is, and who are determined to be good. This is the so-called extraordinary woman in the brothel. As for whoring and sleeping with prostitutes, it is originally willing to enter the lower class, which is not enough to be a lesson. But once tired of wandering and knowing to return, wanting to find an opponent to entrust his dissolute soul, it is also not the first step to turning back. Therefore, we dare not rashly agree to marrying a prostitute; but under special circumstances, it can also be acknowledged.

According to Hong Jun's own account, "the family is poor." Counting from the time he started studying, it has only been three years, and his "financial ability is not yet able to bear the cost of marriage." Then, how was the cost of pleasure-seeking in the past raised? Have you ever stolen from the company? But I want to ask Hong Jun to reflect on himself. If so, then you must work hard in the future and find a way to make up for it. This marriage can only be cut off with heartache, otherwise, once it is discovered, you will have nowhere to stand. Although we dare not "judge the gentleman with the heart of a villain," but for the sake of being loyal to our duties, we do not feel that our words are too direct.

If there is no situation described above, then we can end Hong Jun's past mistakes with the four words "let bygones be bygones." Let's discuss the questions he raised.

The first and second questions at the beginning can only be dealt with by "lying." We know deeply that lying is immoral; but in this stubborn society, seeking people's understanding is useless even if you shout until your throat is hoarse, so there is no better solution other than lying. It is good to say that there is no obvious difference between a prostitute and a woman from a good family! The third question depends on the doctor's assessment, and the procedures should have been resolved before the engagement. Hong Jun neglected it because he was infatuated, which makes us doubt his observation of "knowing what suffering is and being determined to be good." While this big mistake has not been made, I hope Hong Jun will use a calm and sharp eye to observe again. The fourth question does not need to be considered, because the age difference between the couple is three or four years, which is very common and will not cause harm. The fifth question is definitely not possible. Ordinary people say that a prostitute's life is like being in a fire pit; how can one save people from fire and water, and can it be delayed? Moreover, "those who are near vermilion get stained red, and those who are near ink get stained black," and the other party's character is afraid to be affected. As for the economic difficulties, then there is only the method of economizing on food and clothing. Fortunately, the other party is a woman who can endure hardship | As for the sixth question, then it is fundamentally contradictory. We believe that if after consideration, it is considered marriageable, then why say breaking up; if it is considered unmarriageable, then the foundation of love is fundamentally lost, and even if you break up with her, there will be no pain.

A Family of Scholars (Continuation 2) 219

— Wang Zhongxian

"Oh, I understand"! Boss Sang suddenly realized. "He must have gone in last night."

"More than last night, it's like this every night. You just didn't pay attention."

"Strange, strange! The old one is his sister-in-law, and the young one is his niece. Who exactly is his opponent?"

"The old one is thirty-six this year, and the young one is eighteen. His age is right in the middle | I heard that he is exactly twenty-seven years old, and he is suitable for both. If you ask 'who is with whom'? No one can figure it out, unless they themselves." 'You used to get so much grace from the deceased first wife, and Mao Sheng is her beloved child. We see him being bullied by others, can't we think of a way to rescue him?"

(2) The Old Master's Affection is Long, the Wife's Temper is Short

In the Jiangnan region, in the homes of gentry families of the third class or lower, the wall between the first main gate is half rented out to tailors to open clothing shops. However, it is not necessarily because the master is greedy for a few limited rents that the wall is rented out; because the wall of the family, unless there are weddings and funerals, is usually empty and useless. The houses where the masters live, eat, and drink are all deeply hidden behind the third or fourth hall. To take care of the chores at the gate, it is necessary to set up a gatehouse. Gentry of the third class or lower rarely have the opportunity to interact with dignitaries. Hiring a gatekeeper to answer the door only means sitting in the door all day to eat and doze off. Occasionally, when a distinguished guest comes to the door, having someone with sleepy eyes come out to greet them is not very dignified. It is better to rent it out to someone to open a tailor shop, which can earn rent and also take care of the gate, so that thieves cannot covet it. Isn't it convenient?

Sang Aqiang's tailor shop is set up in the wall of someone's house. The surname Xia used to be his old customer, but now he has become his landlord. The Xia family is a big clan in this city. Even with this house owner's branch, there are five direct brothers. The second Master Xia, named Zhongnan, is considered the most capable among his brothers, and he has earned the most family property. (To be continued)

Red-Haired Woman Causes a Scene at the Film Studio 220

— Xun Nan

Clara Bow, the red-haired actress, has always been known for her uninhibited nature since childhood. This time, Fox Film Corporation invited her to film "Wild Girl" (Call Her Savage), precisely to utilize her lively and unrestrained temperament. Unexpectedly, this wonderful person did a wonderful thing. One day at the film studio, she displayed her fierce feminine power and got into a brawl with a female supporting actress. It is feared that this scene might become reality and perhaps even be incorporated as an interesting interlude in "Wild Girl." Because such a genuine fight, this kind of fierce battle with punches and kicks between two women, can only be performed by two extremely shrewish women with deep hatred, and can only happen when they are fighting over a man. Therefore, how could the director lightly let go of such an extraordinary performance when he encountered it?

The story is like this: This day, they were filming an extremely tense scene. In this scene, Clara was supposed to meet her rival, Thelma Todd, in a dance hall. They were supposed to argue and fight due to a disagreement. However, this was all just acting, not real. So Clara and Thelma were both wholeheartedly following the script. But each of them had their own hidden agenda, wanting to show off a little. Thelma later said to people, "This segment is a rare opportunity for me to shine in the entire film, so how could I let it go?"

This is the reason why the two of them were fighting so seriously. What kind of person is Clara? How could she let someone else take the spotlight? Moreover, she is the lead actress of this film, so there is even less room for her to be forgiving. So, when Thelma was wholeheartedly trying to steal the limelight, she stopped acting and started a real fight with Thelma.

Thelma said afterwards, "I don't even know how intense the fight was. But later, I felt that a large clump of my hair had been twisted off by her. After a while, I also had a large clump of red hair in my hand. Later, I kicked with all my might, and she fell to the ground, not moving."

Clara suffered a great loss this time. She received a kick in the stomach from Thelma. As for the extent of her injuries, she refused to admit it herself. It is said that she wrote a letter to Thelma afterwards, saying "We'll meet again someday," but Fox Film Corporation vehemently denied this.

While the two of them were fighting fiercely, creating a chaotic scene, the cameramen were flustered and the director was extremely anxious.

Director Mr. Delen, as if mad and drunk, pulled the cameraman and asked, "Did you capture it?"

"Of course, but it doesn't seem like I was intentionally filming it. I just felt my hand shaking automatically. I really lost myself."

International News

Worth Noting...The US, Germany, and England's Film Industries Join Hands 221

— Ju Xian

丨 Fox, Ufa, and Gaumont

American Fox Film Corporation and German Ufa Film Company have now reached a similar point. The two parties will officially collaborate on productions. The significance of this collaboration is that it is neither Ufa merging with Fox, nor Fox merging with Ufa. It is simply a collaboration on production work, art, and star exchanges. At the same time, Ufa and Fox have also established a relationship with Gaumont British Film Company in London, England. Therefore, Gaumont may also be involved.

The collaboration between Fox and Gaumont also required much effort. Some time ago, American Paramount first entered into cooperation negotiations with the Gaumont authorities. After months of discussions, they finally broke down. After Paramount cancelled the previous agreement, Fox seized the opportunity and easily resolved the issue.

Fox and Ufa are keeping absolute secrecy regarding their collaboration on their works and are still unwilling to announce it publicly. Ufa's representative, Erich Pommer, travels between Europe and America, and rarely tells people about it. In addition to Mr. Pommer, Andre Davin, the production manager traveling between Paris, was also involved in this negotiation. It is also rumored that the productions of the Fox-Ufa collaboration will be filmed in Paris. In addition, Bilian Harvey's recent joining of Fox is a precursor to Ufa's satisfaction with Fox.

This matter was initiated entirely by Ufa. Over the years, they have consulted with various American companies on a way to obtain economic assistance from the American side. Because Ufa felt that it would be better to shoot American versions (note: each country's film shoots versions in foreign languages abroad) than to shoot British versions. The collaboration between Ufa and Gaumont has given them great experience after being screened in the United States. If they cooperate with the United States and use their talent and equipment at the Berlin film studio, it will not be difficult to produce excellent works. With excellent results, it will not be difficult to occupy a

Significant influence in the American market. At first, Ufa wanted to hire American screenwriters and several American stars to go to Germany. This method would of course be welcomed by the United States. However, Ufa's board of directors rejected this plan, believing that the cost was too high. From Fox's perspective, cooperating with Ufa is also extremely cost-effective in terms of economics. Because if Fox did not cooperate, they would have to shoot versions in Germany and compete with Ufa (as all companies do), otherwise they would have to abandon this market. Now that they cooperate with each other, the cost is low and the effectiveness is better. And it can first communicate with various technologies of the German film studio.

Sacrificing for Art 224

— Hong Sun

Karloff's fate, however, Lang Chuck died due to overwork. However, in the past year, Hollywood has discovered a silver star with the same style as Lang Chuck, namely Boris Karloff. He rose to fame after starring in "Frankenstein," but we should know that whenever Karloff plays this character with a strangely beautiful shape that Lang Chuck often played, he must have great patience to resist the pain of forced contortion on the body for a long period of time. When Karloff recently starred in "The Mummy," he worked with long strips of cloth tightly wrapped around him for as long as an hour each time.

Karloff's close friends often advised Karloff to try to do less strenuous work when performing, but he remained silent about it, just like Lang Chuck. He thought that if he could play the role appropriately, he would not feel any pain in his own body. However, in the near future, I am afraid that his muscles will finally be unable to withstand this forced contortion. By then, the film industry will inevitably add another victim.

Do You Know? 225

— Bai Ke

Do you know? Chinese film emperor Jin Yan (although he himself does not admit to being the Chinese film emperor). From December 25th of last year to January 10th of this year, he received a total of 745 Christmas and New Year's cards, of which 562 were sent to him by women. Among these women, according to himself, he doesn't know 98 percent of them at all, but there are also many who were his former classmates, but he can't remember them now. In the 186 Christmas and New Year's cards from men, the opposite is true. He only doesn't know more than ten of them at all, but there are also many who are friends he usually exchanges a few letters with but has never met, accounting for one-fifth. (Retribution)

The Guidelines for Stars 228

— Yuan

"Now that you have entered the film industry, every morning, the gatekeeper of the film studio smiles and opens the door for you. Then you should remember the following golden rules:

"Live in a Spanish-style house on Beverly Hills, but still tell others that it is far less comfortable than living in a plank house in your hometown."

"Try to get married and hold a grand and solemn wedding."

"Try to get divorced, but you must firmly declare that you and your ex-husband are still 'close friends'."

"Uphold the spirit of democracy and casually talk to the electrical workers, prop workers, and all the people in charge in the film studio at any time."

"Be especially intimate with visitors, ask them to keep the conversation a secret: do not publish it in the newspaper, although the news they get has already been known to others, you still have to make them feel that this is an unpublished secret conversation."

"For the relationship with relatives and old friends, you must make people see that you 'remember the old days' and that you have not forgotten poverty and humbleness."

"In addition, there are many things that should or should not be done, but if you follow the above, it will be enough for you to ask for whatever you want and eat endlessly!"

"The above eight rules will never lose their effectiveness!"

Tianyi Broadcasting Station Trial Broadcast Program 229

— Xi

Tianyi Film Company and China Radio Research Institute jointly operate a radio station, which has been approved by the Ministry of Communications and issued Permit No. 1. It is designated to use 1140 kilocycles. The broadcasting studio is located inside the Tianyi Company. It has now been fully equipped. The broadcasting program is hosted by the company's male and female stars. It is scheduled to officially open on the 26th of this month, with trial broadcasts starting on the 20th. The programs include Yuan Meiyun's "June Snow," Chen Jingfang's "Tuberose," Shu Lijuan's "Fengyang Flower Drum," Shao Suxia and Chen Qixia's "Si Lang Visits His Mother," Luye's "Spring Rain Just Cleared," and Fu Guifeng's "Su San's Escort," etc. In the future, after the official opening, the major stars will take turns broadcasting, and the programs will be even more exciting, it is said.

"Match King" (15) 230

— Translated by Xi Meng

Eric, with a face haggard and on the verge of death from worry, saw Paul and asked in surprise:

"Where did you go? I was almost going crazy."

"I told you, don't worry," Paul said calmly. "I'll take care of everything."

"But where are we going to find 40 million in cash?"

Paul shrugged his shoulders and said unhurriedly:

"I'll take these Italian treasury bonds to Wall Street in New York, are you afraid I can't sell them for money?"

"Italian treasury bonds...Italian treasury bonds?" Eric said in surprise. "Didn't you already sell them long ago?"

"Eric," Paul said to him calmly, "You still don't know about me. What you know is really very little. When I come back from New York, I will tell you in detail. You don't need to worry now... Now I ask you to send a telegram to Muerena, telling her to meet me in New York next Monday. Tell her that I must meet her."

Eric sighed a sigh of relief and said admiringly:

"Paul, you are really unpredictable." After he finished speaking, his heart added even more admiration.

Paul smiled, took out a photo of Muerena from the drawer, looked at it for a while, and closed his eyes. He held the photo of Muerena against his chest. Inside his chest were the already dead Scallatti's treasury bonds, which she had completely forgotten.

He arrived in New York and hurried to the hotel to meet Muerena. While he was at sea, he had already communicated with her once by radio, saying that she could only stay in New York for one day. So when he arrived at the hotel, he had been waiting for a long time.

"Mattie!" He said one word in a hoarse voice, and couldn't continue. His eyes were full of adoration. She was even more beautiful than before. He looked at her and his heart was jumping uncontrollably. He hurriedly walked over.

But he was not allowed to get close to her, and was rejected.

Paul was too happy, so he didn't notice that Muerena's attitude had changed.

"Mattie!" he said softly. "Only now can I finally get what I want. I have borrowed a large sum of money, so that I can get rid of all the chores from now on and spend all day with you, never to be separated. I have planned everything. You don't need to film movies anymore.

Mattie, I want to marry you as my wife." As he said this, he wanted to hug her, but she opened up again.
